=========================================================
SECTION 2 — PURETASK PLATFORM RULES (ULTRA EXPANDED, FULL CANON)
=========================================================
PureTask is a trust-driven marketplace with strict rules designed to protect:

clients

cleaners

the platform integrity

the brand reputation

This section outlines every behavioral, operational, and safety rule governing the marketplace.

It is divided into:

Global Platform Rules

Client Rules

Cleaner Rules

Reliability System Rules

Check-in / GPS Rules

Photo Proof Rules

Job Behavior & Professionalism Rules

Cancellation Rules

Dispute Rules

Fraud Prevention Rules

Safety & Conduct Rules

Escalation & Enforcement Framework

Fairness & Accountability Principles

Evidence Standards

Edge Case Handling

Let’s go deep.

---------------------------------------------------------
1. GLOBAL PLATFORM RULES (Apply to Everyone)
These rules apply to both clients and cleaners:

All communication must occur within the app.

Payment can only be processed via credits + escrow.

Jobs must be verified using GPS check-in/out.

All job completion must include before/after photos.

Both sides must follow professional conduct.

No off-platform transactions are allowed.

All disputes are resolved using evidence only.

Personal data must be protected.

PureTask may intervene in case of safety issues.

Fraud is grounds for immediate and permanent ban.

These are foundational.

---------------------------------------------------------
2. CLIENT RULES (Ultra Expanded)
2.1 Booking Rules
Clients must:

provide accurate address

select correct cleaning type

have enough credits in wallet

confirm the date/time

ensure access to the home is possible

Clients cannot:

book cleaners for illegal, unsafe, or non-cleaning tasks

misrepresent the size or condition of the home

2.2 Approval Rules
Clients must:

review photos before approving

approve or dispute within the designated time window (usually 24 hours)

provide specific reasoning if disputing

Clients cannot:

refuse approval without valid reason

delay reviews excessively to inconvenience cleaner payments

2.3 Conduct Rules
Clients must:

be respectful

provide clean and safe working conditions

avoid inappropriate behavior

avoid harassment or discrimination

avoid entering cleaner’s personal space unnecessarily

Clients cannot:

attempt to intimidate cleaners

contact cleaners outside the app

make inappropriate comments

2.4 Cancellation Rules (client-triggered)
PureTask must enforce:

Cancellation >24 hours = full credit return

Cancellation <24 hours = partial fee

Cancellation <3 hours = higher fee

No-show by client = 100% job charge (cleaner still paid)

These rules protect cleaner income.

2.5 Client Violations
Automatic actions:

first issue → warning

repeated issues → account review

safety violations → immediate suspension

harassment → permanent ban

---------------------------------------------------------
3. CLEANER RULES (Ultra Expanded)
Cleaners are independent professionals but must comply with platform rules to ensure safety & trust.

3.1 Availability & Acceptance Rules
Cleaners must:

accept only jobs they can attend

maintain updated availability

not cancel last-minute unless emergency

only accept within their travel radius

Cleaners cannot:

accept jobs as placeholders

consistently decline hour before

ignore assigned jobs

3.2 Check-in Rules (Critical)
Cleaners must:

check in within 200 meters of the home

use real GPS (no spoofing)

check in upon arrival, not earlier or later

If check-in doesn’t work:

cleaner must troubleshoot

ensure location services are enabled

retry before contacting support

3.3 Photo Proof Rules (Extremely Important)
Cleaners must upload:

before photos (minimum 2 angles per area)

after photos (matching angles)

Photos must be:

clear

well-lit

not blurry

taken on the spot

not reused

not edited

Missing or poor photo sets → reliability penalty.

3.4 Conduct & Professionalism
Cleaners must:

behave respectfully

not steal or damage property

not smoke inside

not bring guests

not use client supplies unless approved

not take personal calls throughout the job

respect personal belongings

3.5 Reliability Rule Summary
Cleaners must:

arrive on time

check in properly

upload complete proof

stay for full booked duration

communicate professionally

3.6 Payout & Earnings Rules
Cleaners:

earn credits after job approval

can cash out weekly

can use instant payout if eligible

cannot negotiate off-platform fees

cannot request cash

3.7 Cleaner Violations
Instant penalties for:

no-show (-50 reliability)

last-minute cancellation (-25 reliability)

missing photos (-15)

fake photos (-100, possible ban)

GPS fraud (permanent ban)

harassment or safety violation (permanent ban)

---------------------------------------------------------
4. RELIABILITY SYSTEM RULES (CORE OF PLATFORM)
Every cleaner has a reliability score (0–100).

It is controlled by:

attendance

photo compliance

ratings

cancellations

disputes

check-in accuracy

Positive Events:
+20 = On-time arrival
+15 = Perfect photo proof
+10 = 5-star rating
+5 = early acceptance of job

Negative Events:
-50 = no-show
-30 = incomplete job
-25 = late cancellation
-20 = late arrival
-15 = missing photos
-10 = messy or unclear photos
-5 = client complaint (non-dispute)

Tier Boundaries:
Bronze = 0–69

Silver = 70–84

Gold = 85–94

Platinum = 95+

Tiers unlock:

earning percentages

job visibility

priority ranking

---------------------------------------------------------
5. GPS & CHECK-IN RULES (Absolute Requirements)
Check-in/out is the heart of trust.

Rules:

Check-in must occur at the job location.

Must occur when arriving, not before.

Must be triggered through the app, not third-party tools.

Photos cannot be uploaded without check-in.

GPS spoofing results in immediate ban.

Wi-Fi-based GPS manipulation is prohibited.

Tolerance:

distance threshold: up to 200 meters

time threshold: within 15 minutes of scheduled time

---------------------------------------------------------
6. PHOTO PROOF SYSTEM RULES (STRICT)
PureTask requires undeniable evidence of work.

Requirements:

minimum 2 angles per room (before & after)

consistent angles

no movement of camera significantly

lighting must be adequate

after photos must match before photo framing

no photo filters

no collage photos

no screenshots

no uploading photos taken in past

EXIF anomalies may trigger review

Automatic flags:

repeated identical photos

too-dark or blurry images

mismatched angles

metadata issues

---------------------------------------------------------
7. JOB BEHAVIOR RULES (CLEANER PROFESSIONALISM)
Cleaners must:

greet client if present

ask clarifying questions

follow provided instructions

work diligently

avoid personal calls

not take long breaks

not leave early

not invite outsiders

Clients must:

allow cleaners safe access

provide instructions

maintain a respectful environment

avoid hovering or interfering excessively

---------------------------------------------------------
8. CANCELLATION RULES (FULL LOGIC)
8.1 Client Cancellations
24 hours → 100% credit refund

<24 hours → fee charged (for cleaner inconvenience)

<3 hours → higher penalty

no client present (locked out) → treated as client no-show

8.2 Cleaner Cancellations
24 hours → no penalty

<24 hours → -15 to -25 reliability

<3 hours → -25 to -40 reliability

no-show → -50 + temporary suspension

8.3 Platform Cancellations
If due to:

emergencies

safety violations

natural disasters

→ no penalties applied.

---------------------------------------------------------
9. DISPUTE RULES (EVIDENCE-FIRST SYSTEM)
PureTask disputes rely entirely on:

before/after photos

check-in data

cleaner’s notes

client’s notes

job scope

Clients can dispute for:

incomplete cleaning

poor cleaning quality

missing areas

insufficient time spent

Cleaners can dispute if:

client requests extra unpaid work

client tries to exploit the approval process

Outcomes:

approve full payment

partial refund

full refund

cleaner penalty depending on fault

Dispute resolution time: typically 24–48 hours.

---------------------------------------------------------
10. FRAUD PREVENTION RULES
Forbidden actions:

For Cleaners:
uploading reused photos

starting check-in away from job location

leaving early after checking in

working far less time than claimed

faking after photos without cleaning

colluding with clients

attempting off-platform deals

For Clients:
falsely disputing legitimate work

requesting services not included

threatening negative reviews

colluding with cleaners to exploit system

Immediate ban for:

GPS spoofing

fake photos

aggressive fraud attempts

---------------------------------------------------------
11. SAFETY & CONDUCT RULES
Cleaners:
no harassment

no discrimination

no theft

no entering private spaces unless asked

no illegal substances

no unsafe behavior

Clients:
no harassment

no unwanted advances

no unsafe environments

no intoxication making environment risky

Safety violations = instant suspension pending review.

---------------------------------------------------------
12. ESCALATION & ENFORCEMENT FRAMEWORK
Level 1: Warning
minor issue

missing photos once

unclear communication

Level 2: Reliability Penalty
repeated small issues

late arrivals

unclear photos

Level 3: Temporary Suspension
repeated no-shows

repeated disputes

trust issues

safety concerns

Level 4: Permanent Ban
fraud

theft

harassment

GPS spoofing

falsified photos

---------------------------------------------------------
13. FAIRNESS & ACCOUNTABILITY PRINCIPLES
PureTask must always:

treat both sides neutrally

base decisions on evidence

follow consistent rules

avoid emotional bias

support safe dialogue

document all interactions

Cleaners are independent contractors; clients are platform users.
Rules must respect both roles equally.

---------------------------------------------------------
14. EVIDENCE STANDARDS (DETAILED)
Photo evidence must be:

timestamped

clear

unmixed with other jobs

accurate to space

GPS evidence must be:

from device

unmodified

consistent with known checkpoints

Client statements are secondary to:

Photos

GPS data

Cleaner notes

Disputes are NOT emotional debates — they are evidence cases.

---------------------------------------------------------
15. EDGE CASE RULES (FULL)
If cleaner forgets to check in:
must contact support immediately

platform may allow manual override at cost to reliability

If client is not home:
cleaner may proceed depending on instructions

if no access → client no-show

If job takes longer:
client must approve additional time

cleaner must document the reason

If property is unsafe:
cleaner must leave

platform is notified

client may be suspended

If the home is overwhelmingly dirty:
cleaner may request job cancel with documentation

=========================================================
3A — BOOKING SYSTEM (ULTRA-EXPANDED CANON)
=========================================================
The Booking System is one of the core pillars of PureTask.
It must be:

simple

reliable

trust-building

transparent

frictionless

cleanly structured

It is not just a calendar → it is the mechanism that coordinates:

credits

cleaners

GPS logic

availability

time estimation

job creation

escrow

notifications

automations

pre-job compliance

Below is the official Canon-level description.

---------------------------------------------------------
1. PURPOSE OF THE BOOKING SYSTEM
PureTask’s booking system must:

allow clients to book a cleaning in minutes

match clients with qualified cleaners

place credits into escrow automatically

configure time & scope of the job

ensure the cleaner receives accurate job details

ensure trust via transparency & clarity

prevent double bookings

comply with all reliability & tier rules

prepare the job for check-in / proof workflows

---------------------------------------------------------
2. BOOKING FLOW OVERVIEW (CLIENT SIDE)
This is the full sequence:

Step 1: Enter Address
Client inputs:

street address

unit number

gate code (optional)

parking instructions

The address must validate via:

Google Places API

geolocation check

home profile record creation

Step 2: Select Service Type
Options may include:

Standard Cleaning

Deep Cleaning

Move-in / Move-out

Custom Instructions

Each service type adjusts:

estimated duration

recommended cleaner tier

base expectations

Step 3: Home Profile
Client enters:

number of bedrooms

number of bathrooms

home size (sq ft optional)

pets (yes/no)

clutter level (light, normal, heavy)

This feeds:

time estimate

cleaner recommendations

dispute validation data

future bookings memory

Step 4: Choose Date & Time
Calendar logic shows only:

cleaner-available slots

same-day or next-day availability (if supported)

recommended times based on cleaner density

Rules:

cannot book less than 2 hours from now

cannot book more than X days into future (configurable)

Step 5: Cleaner Selection
Clients can:

browse available cleaners

view rates

view reliability score

view reviews

view tier badge

view travel distance

Cleaner ordering algorithm:

highest tier first

highest reliability

shortest distance

best match for job type

cleaner availability

If client chooses “Auto-Select Cleaner,” system selects the top-ranked match.

Step 6: Credit Requirement Check
System calculates estimated hours × cleaner's tier rate.

If insufficient credits:

client is prompted to add credits

wallet is topped up via card

credits go into escrow

No booking moves forward without escrow.

Step 7: Final Confirmation
Client reviews:

job time

cleaner assigned

address

special instructions

estimated hours

escrow credits held

Client taps “Confirm Booking”.

---------------------------------------------------------
3. BOOKING FLOW (CLEANER SIDE)
Cleaners see incoming jobs via the Job Feed.

A job becomes visible when:

client has fully confirmed

credits are in escrow

cleaner fits availability rules

Cleaner views:

job location

date/time

estimated duration

client instructions

compensation preview

projected tier-boost opportunities

Cleaner actions:

Accept

Decline

Ask for clarification

If cleaner declines, system selects next best match.

---------------------------------------------------------
4. CREDIT ESCROW LOGIC DURING BOOKING
Credits are immediately:

deducted from client wallet

placed in escrow

assigned to the job

locked until job approval

Escrow protects:

client (they don’t pay until approval)

cleaner (credits guaranteed if work is done)

If the cleaner cancels → escrow unlocks
If the job is canceled properly → credits returned per policy

---------------------------------------------------------
5. REAL-TIME AVAILABILITY LOGIC
The system calculates availability by checking:

5.1 Cleaner Calendar
their declared hours

blocked days

scheduled jobs

travel time

5.2 Travel Buffer
Cleaners must have minimum 30 minutes between jobs.

Automatic travel-time calculation is based on:

distance from previous job

cleaner’s chosen transport mode

5.3 Tier-Based Availability
Higher-tier cleaners get:

early visibility

prime slots

privileged matching

---------------------------------------------------------
6. ESTIMATED TIME CALCULATION LOGIC
Time estimation uses:

number of bedrooms

number of bathrooms

clutter level

service type

cleaner tier speed multiplier

Example baseline:

1 bedroom: 30 minutes

1 bathroom: 20 minutes

kitchen: 30 minutes

living areas: 40 minutes

System adjusts up/down based on:

home size

cleaner efficiency data

historic job completion times

This estimate powers:

escrow calculation

payout expectation

cleaner scheduling

reliability scoring (duration compliance)

---------------------------------------------------------
7. BOOKING CONFIRMATION STATES
After booking:

Client sees:

“Your cleaner will check in when they arrive.”

upcoming job timetable

cancel/reschedule button (until cutoff time)

Cleaner sees:

“Job Confirmed”

countdown timer

directions button

check-in button (disabled until arrival)

---------------------------------------------------------
8. RESCHEDULING RULES
Clients may reschedule if:

24 hrs before

cleaner is available at new time

escrow remains intact

If cleaner unavailable → fallback cleaner search occurs.

If no cleaner available → client must choose different time.

---------------------------------------------------------
9. EDGE CASE HANDLING
9.1 Cleaner Accepts, Then Cancels
System triggers:

find replacement cleaner

notify client immediately

reliability penalty for cleaner

9.2 No Cleaner Accepts
job is canceled

credits refunded

client pushed recommendations

9.3 Client Insufficient Credits
Booking cannot proceed until wallet topped up.

9.4 Address Not Found
User must correct the address or place manual map pin.

---------------------------------------------------------
10. BACKEND ENTITIES & DATA STORED
Job object stores:

job_id

client_id

cleaner_id

home profile

service type

estimated duration

scheduled start time

booking created timestamp

escrow amount

job status

cancellation history

automations triggered

---------------------------------------------------------
11. AUTOMATIONS TRIGGERED DURING BOOKING
Automation 1: On Booking Created
send client confirmation

notify cleaner pool

lock credits into escrow

write job into scheduling system

Automation 2: On Cleaner Accept
assign job officially

freeze calendar slot

notify client

Automation 3: On Booking Reminder
Sent:

24 hours before

1 hour before

cleaner’s arrival notification

Automation 4: On Reschedule
update cleaner schedule

recalc travel time

update reminders

---------------------------------------------------------
12. COMPLETE BOOKING LIFECYCLE SUMMARY
Client chooses → system estimates → escrow created → cleaner accepts → confirmation → job day → check-in → completion → proof → approval → payout.

The booking system is the beginning of the entire job lifecycle.

=========================================================
3C — WALLET & CREDIT SYSTEM (ULTRA-EXPANDED CANON)
=========================================================
The PureTask Wallet and Credit System is the financial backbone of the marketplace.

It ensures:

Clients pay upfront safely

Cleaners get paid fairly only when job is approved

Platform prevents chargebacks, cancellations, and disputes

Cash never moves directly between client ↔ cleaner

This creates a trusted, controlled, fraud-resistant payment environment.

This section defines:

credit lifecycle

wallet structure

escrow logic

credit → earnings conversion

refund system

dispute integrations

instant payout rules

admin override rules

fraud protections

UI flows

automations

Let’s break it down.

---------------------------------------------------------
1. PURPOSE OF THE CREDIT SYSTEM
Why PureTask uses credits instead of dollars:

✔ Trust
Clients load credits → credits go into escrow → only released after approval.

✔ Cleaner Protection
Credits guarantee cleaners get paid for real work before the job even starts.

✔ Predictable Product UX
A credit system avoids:

partial card charges

variable hour billing surprises

timing mismatches

payout transaction failures

✔ Dispute-Friendly
If a dispute occurs:

credits can be partially refunded

partially released

held until resolution

✔ Legal + Classification Protection
Credits help maintain the marketplace structure, not employment structure.

---------------------------------------------------------
2. CREDIT LIFECYCLE (START → END)
This is how credits flow through the system:

Step 1 — Client Purchases Credits
Client enters credit amount

Stripe processes payment

Credits instantly appear in wallet

Step 2 — Client Books a Job
Credits required for estimated time × cleaner rate

Credits are moved into Escrow Hold

Wallet balance decreases

Step 3 — Cleaner Completes Job + Uploads Proof
After job → cleaner submits photos

Client is notified

Step 4 — Client Approves or Disputes
If approved:

Escrow credits → move to Cleaner Earnings Ledger

If disputed:

Escrow credits remain frozen

Admin reviews

Step 5 — Payout
Weekly payout: automatically released to cleaner’s bank

Instant payout: processed immediately (fee applies)

Step 6 — Remaining Credits Stay in Wallet
Client can:

book another job

refund (special cases only)

This cycle repeats for every job.

---------------------------------------------------------
3. WALLET STRUCTURE (DATA MODEL)
The wallet consists of 4 balance types:

1. Available Balance
Credits client can use for bookings.

2. Escrow Balance
Credits locked for assigned jobs.

3. Pending Refunds
Credits waiting for dispute resolution or partial returns.

4. Promotional / Bonus Credits (optional)
Used for:

new user bonuses

cleaner referral rewards

email marketing promotions

Promotional credits:

cannot be cashed out

do not convert to earnings

expire after X days

---------------------------------------------------------
4. CREDIT PURCHASE FLOW (CLIENT)
Step 1: User chooses credit pack
pre-set amounts ($50, $100, $250, $500)

or custom amount

Step 2: Payment processed via Stripe
card authorization

fraud scoring

risk evaluation

success → credits added

failure → user notified

Step 3: Wallet updated
transaction ID saved

credit ledger updated

Step 4: Notification
“Your credits are now available.”

Refundable?
Credits themselves are not refundable unless:

job never happened

dispute ruled in client’s favor

extreme exception (fraud, double charge, etc.)

---------------------------------------------------------
5. ESCROW SYSTEM (CRITICAL)
When a client books a job:

the required credits are moved from Available → Escrow

these credits remain locked

neither client nor cleaner can access them

admin cannot manually release them (must follow rules)

Escrow prevents:

unpaid jobs

cancellation abuse

failure to complete payments

Escrow is released only when:

✔ Job is approved
✔ Dispute is resolved
✔ Policy-driven partial payout is executed
✔ Job is cancelled by platform

---------------------------------------------------------
6. CREDIT TO EARNINGS CONVERSION (CLEANER SIDE)
When a job is approved:

escrow credits convert into a cash-equivalent earning

conversion is instant

cleaner sees earnings in their Earnings Ledger

BUT money is not paid yet.
The earning is scheduled for payout.

Example Conversion:
Client pays 300 credits
Cleaner earns 300 credits → equivalent to $300 (minus PureTask fee)

PureTask Fee Structure (example):
Bronze cleaners: 30% fee

Silver: 25%

Gold: 20%

Platinum: 15%

So cleaners have incentive to increase reliability and tier.

---------------------------------------------------------
7. CREDIT REFUNDS & ADJUSTMENTS
Credits are refunded in these cases:

1. Client Cancels >24 Hours Before Job
→ 100% returned

2. Client Cancels <24 Hours
→ partial refund (policy-based)

3. Cleaner Cancels
→ full refund
→ no penalty for client

4. Dispute Resolved in Client Favor
Possible outcomes:

partial refund

full refund

corrective refund

5. Platform Error
Full refund if:

system glitch

double charge

incorrect time estimate

Refunds ALWAYS return to CREDITS, not money (except special exceptions).

---------------------------------------------------------
8. CREDIT EXPIRATION RULES (OPTIONAL)
PureTask may or may not enforce expiration depending on business model.

Standard recommended rule:

credits expire 18–24 months after purchase

BUT promotional credits expire sooner:

60–90 days

Expiration is:

clearly communicated

visible in wallet

auto-notified 30 days before expiring

---------------------------------------------------------
9. FRAUD PROTECTION (FINANCIAL)
This is critical.

9.1 Suspicious Credit Purchases
Triggers:

multiple cards

mismatched billing addresses

rapid purchase attempts

prepaid or disposable cards

high dispute rate

Action:

temporary wallet freeze

booking restrictions

manual review

9.2 Cleaner Fraud Detection
Examples:

coordinating with clients to simulate jobs

uploading staged photos

fake addresses

System blocks:

credit flow

payouts

account status is reviewed

9.3 Chargeback Protection
If a client disputes a credit purchase with bank:

credits are removed from wallet

any jobs funded with those credits are frozen

cleaner payouts paused

account may be suspended

Credit system protects cleaners because jobs cannot be funded by invalid payments.

---------------------------------------------------------
10. CLIENT WALLET UI / UX
Client sees:

Wallet Overview
Available credits

Credits in escrow

Expiring credits

Credit purchase button

Credit history

Detailed View
transaction list

booking-specific holds

refunds processed

promotions

receipts

Call-To-Action
“Add Credits”

“Buy More Credits Before Booking”

“Credits Held for Upcoming Job”

---------------------------------------------------------
11. CLEANER EARNINGS UI / UX
Cleaners see:

Earnings Breakdown
job-based earnings

upcoming payout

instant payout eligibility

fees deducted

bonuses earned

Graphs
weekly earnings

monthly totals

hourly earning averages

Transaction History
job earnings

payout transfers

instant payout fees

Payout Controls
“Request Instant Payout”

“Connect Bank Account”

“View Payout Statements”

---------------------------------------------------------
12. ADMIN OVERRIDE RULES
Admins can:

adjust credits manually

release escrow manually

refund credits

reverse refunds

freeze wallets

review suspicious activity

correct mistakes

Admins cannot:

grant arbitrary payouts without reason

bypass Stripe Connect compliance

convert credits to money directly

Every admin action logs:

admin_id

timestamp

justification

---------------------------------------------------------
13. AUTOMATIONS INSIDE THE CREDIT SYSTEM
Automation 1 — Low Credit Warning
When wallet < next booking estimate:
→ notify client to add credits

Automation 2 — Credit Hold On Booking
Immediate move to escrow

Automation 3 — Expiring Credit Reminder
Sent 30 days / 7 days before expiration

Automation 4 — Dispute Freeze
Escrow locked until resolution

Automation 5 — Payout Eligibility
If cleaner meets rules:
→ mark earnings ready for payout

---------------------------------------------------------
14. EDGE CASES
Client buys too few credits
→ booking blocked until topped up

Client buys credits but card charge fails
→ credits removed
→ notification sent

Cleaner completed job but client disappears
→ auto-approval after X hours
→ escrow released

Refund causes negative balance
→ wallet locked
→ cannot book until resolved

Perfect — continuing with SECTION 3D, one of the most important and technically detailed modules of the entire PureTask platform.

This section describes the entire lifecycle of a job from the moment it's booked until payout is completed.

It governs:

job creation

check-in

work duration

photo proof

job completion

disputes

finalization

This is the operational heart of PureTask.

=========================================================
3D — JOB LIFECYCLE & APPROVAL SYSTEM (ULTRA-EXPANDED CANON)
=========================================================
A PureTask job passes through 12 distinct phases.

Each phase contains:

UI states

backend logic

automations

rules

safety conditions

status transitions

failure modes

timestamps

data entries

notifications

We will go through each one.

---------------------------------------------------------
1. JOB LIFECYCLE OVERVIEW — THE 12 PHASES
Job Created

Cleaner Assigned

Pre-Job State (Upcoming)

Cleaner Travel

Check-In (GPS Validation)

Active Job / In-Progress State

Before Photos Submitted

Cleaning Work

After Photos Submitted

Job Presented to Client for Review

Client Approval OR Dispute

Finalization → Payout

This ensures fairness and transparency.

---------------------------------------------------------
2. PHASE 1 — JOB CREATED
Triggered when:

client completes booking

credits successfully placed into escrow

System logs:

job_id

client_id

cleaner candidate list

estimated duration

required credits

address

special notes

Automations:

Send client confirmation

Notify cleaners

Freeze credits into escrow

Add to cleaner calendars (tentative)

Status: JOB_CREATED

---------------------------------------------------------
3. PHASE 2 — CLEANER ASSIGNED
A cleaner is assigned when:

cleaner accepts manually

OR system auto-selects best cleaner

System then:

updates job owner → cleaner_id

confirms cleaner eligibility

removes job from other cleaner feeds

locks the slot

sends confirmation to client & cleaner

Status: CLEANER_ASSIGNED

---------------------------------------------------------
4. PHASE 3 — PRE-JOB STATE (“Upcoming Job”)
This is the window between assignment and arrival.

Cleaner UI:
job date/time

directions

job instructions

parking notes

check-in button (disabled)

Client UI:
cleaner details

cancellation window

timeline

phone masked number (optional)

instructions editable

Automations:

24-hour reminder

1-hour reminder

cleaner travel reminder

Status: UPCOMING

---------------------------------------------------------
5. PHASE 4 — CLEANER TRAVEL
Triggered automatically X minutes before job start (ex: 30 minutes).

Cleaner sees:

“It's time to head to your job.”

directions via maps

Client sees:

“Your cleaner is on the way.”

GPS is NOT tracked during travel (privacy + simplicity).
Only check-in location matters.

Status remains UPCOMING.

---------------------------------------------------------
6. PHASE 5 — CHECK-IN (GPS VALIDATION)
This is one of the MOST IMPORTANT steps in the entire PureTask system.

Cleaner must:

Arrive at job location

Be physically within geofence (200 meters recommended)

Open app

Tap “Check In”

The system validates:

GPS accuracy

Distance to home location

Timestamp vs start time

Device integrity (spoof check)

Network reliability

If GPS fails:

cleaner receives troubleshooting steps

must retry

can contact support

If spoofing is detected:

immediate account freeze

admin review

job canceled

client refunded

Once validated:

job moves to IN_PROGRESS

job start time = check-in timestamp

Client receives:
“Your cleaner has arrived and checked in.”

---------------------------------------------------------
7. PHASE 6 — ACTIVE JOB (IN-PROGRESS STATE)
Once check-in is confirmed:

Cleaner UI shows:

timer

instructions

safety info

expected end time

Client sees:

cleaning in progress

check-in time

expected finish window

Backend records:

exact start time

timestamps for photos

session events

Status: IN_PROGRESS

---------------------------------------------------------
8. PHASE 7 — BEFORE PHOTOS SUBMITTED
Before cleaning begins, the cleaner must upload before photos.

Rules:

minimum 2 angles per room

consistent framing

no filters

complete coverage

light must be adequate

System evaluates:

clarity

brightness

metadata integrity

Cleaner cannot proceed to “after photos” until all before photos are uploaded.

Status remains IN_PROGRESS.

---------------------------------------------------------
9. PHASE 8 — CLEANING WORK
Cleaner completes cleaning.

During job:

timer continues

cleaner may pause briefly

cleaner may add notes (ex: broken items encountered, instructions issues)

Client sees:

nothing new — just that job is ongoing

System stores:

time elapsed

any changes (like added rooms, extra time requested)

Automations possible:

“You've reached 80% of estimated time.”

“Would you like to request additional time?”

---------------------------------------------------------
10. PHASE 9 — AFTER PHOTOS SUBMITTED
When cleaning is complete:

Cleaner must:

upload after photos

match same angles as before

confirm job areas are completed

attach optional final notes for the client

System runs:

photo analysis

metadata comparison

quality scoring

If poor quality:

cleaner gets warning

reliability penalty applies

Client receives:
“Your job photos are ready for review.”

Status changes to AWAITING_REVIEW.

---------------------------------------------------------
11. PHASE 10 — REVIEW & APPROVAL FLOW (Client)
Client now reviews:

before photos

after photos

cleaner notes

check-in time

duration

hourly rate

total credit cost

Client can choose:

⭐ Approve Job
→ releases credits
→ moves to payout queue

⚠️ Request Fix / Correction
Client describes issue.
Cleaner notified.
Cleaner may revisit or provide justification.

❗ Open Dispute
Triggers dispute workflow.

⏳ If client is unresponsive
Auto-approval occurs after:

24 hours (recommended)

OR configurable time window

This protects cleaner payouts.

---------------------------------------------------------
12. PHASE 11 — DISPUTE (IF CHOSEN)

Admin sees:

photos

cleaner statements

history of similar jobs

Outcomes:

cleaner penalty

client penalty

Once resolved:

escrow released accordingly

job completed

---------------------------------------------------------

Cleaner earnings become:

Job Status: COMPLETED

Cleaner sees:

earnings added

Client sees:

job receipt

rating prompt

=========================================================
3E — PAYOUT SYSTEM (ULTRA-EXPANDED CANON)
=========================================================
The Payout System governs the movement of cleaner earnings → real money.
It is tightly integrated with:

Stripe Connect

reliability engine

dispute engine

escrow logic

weekly payout schedule

instant payout module

fraud detection

admin manual controls

PureTask cannot afford errors in payout logic, so every rule below is designed to ensure fairness, speed, accuracy, and compliance.

---------------------------------------------------------
1. PURPOSE OF PAYOUT SYSTEM
PureTask’s payout system ensures:

Cleaners are paid accurately

Payments comply with legal and financial rules

Escrow and dispute logic are respected

Fraudulent payouts are prevented

Payment delays are minimized

Transparency is maintained

Cleaners trust the platform

PureTask remains compliant with Stripe Connect, tax laws, and contractor classification rules

---------------------------------------------------------
2. PAYOUT FRAMEWORK OVERVIEW
A payout flows through five stages:

Earnings Added (after job approval)

Eligible for Payout (midweek)

Payout Scheduled (weekly or instant)

Stripe Transfer Initiated

Transfer Settled (funds received in bank)

Each stage has:

validations

automations

logs

timestamps

backup protections

---------------------------------------------------------
3. PAYOUT METHODS (TWO OPTIONS)
PureTask supports two payout methods:

(1) Weekly Automatic Payouts
runs once per week

includes all eligible earnings

processed via Stripe Connect

sent directly to cleaner bank account

(2) Instant Payouts
available for eligible cleaners

triggers immediately

fee deducted (configurable, ex: 1–3%)

uses Stripe’s “Instant Payout” system

must meet risk thresholds to be allowed

---------------------------------------------------------
4. WHAT COUNTS AS EARNINGS?
Credits convert to earnings ONLY when:

job has been approved

OR dispute resolved in cleaner favor

OR partial payout awarded

If job is not approved:

funds remain in escrow

not eligible for payout

Refunds do NOT count as earnings.

---------------------------------------------------------
5. ELIGIBILITY RULES FOR PAYOUT
Cleaners MUST meet all criteria:

Rule 1 — Valid Stripe Connect Account
must have completed identity verification

must have linked bank account

must be fully compliant

Cleaner cannot be paid through:

Venmo

PayPal

Zelle

cash

any non-Stripe methods

Rule 2 — No Active Fraud Flags
If flagged, payout is frozen.

Rule 3 — Dispute-Free Jobs Only
Jobs under dispute → not eligible.

Rule 4 — Minimum Earnings Threshold
Example:

minimum $25–50 for weekly payout

Instant payout may require:

minimum $10

Rule 5 — Completed Job Requirements
Cleaner must have:

valid check-in

full photo proof

completed checklist

Missing any requirement → earnings withheld pending review.

---------------------------------------------------------
6. WEEKLY AUTOMATIC PAYOUTS (FULL LOGIC)
Schedule:
Runs every Monday at 00:00 UTC (configurable).

Process:
system identifies all eligible earnings

batch compiles earnings summary

sends payout request to Stripe

logs payout ID

updates cleaner earnings dashboard

sends notification:

“Your weekly payout has been sent.”

Settlement Time:
typically 2 business days

varies by bank

holidays may delay

If payout fails:
Stripe returns a failure code

PureTask notifies cleaner

cleaner must update bank info

Common failure reasons:

incorrect account number

closed account

name mismatch

risk hold

---------------------------------------------------------
7. INSTANT PAYOUT SYSTEM (FULL LOGIC)
Instant payouts allow cleaners to cash out immediately.

Eligibility:
reliability score ≥ 85

no disputes in last 7 days

no fraud flags

fully verified Stripe account

balance above minimum threshold

Process:
cleaner taps “Instant Payout”

fee is deducted

Stripe is triggered to send money instantly

money usually arrives in minutes

logs created

Restrictions:
maximum instant payout frequency (ex: 3/day)

max daily payout amount

cannot include disputed earnings

cannot include escrow funds

Fee Example:
1.75% of total instant payout

or minimum $0.50 per transaction

---------------------------------------------------------
8. FRAUD HOLDS & RISK MANAGEMENT
To protect clients and PureTask, certain conditions freeze payouts:

Fraud Triggers:
abnormal GPS patterns

repeated missing photo sets

client reports of incomplete work

identity mismatch

bank account mismatch

device spoofing

unusually high earnings spikes

multiple disputes filed in a short time

evidence of collusion with clients

Actions Taken:
payout temporarily frozen

review opened

cleaner notified

If confirmed fraud:

funds returned to clients

cleaner permanently banned

authorities notified (if necessary)

---------------------------------------------------------
9. DISPUTE INTEGRATION WITH PAYOUT SYSTEM
If a dispute is opened:

entire job payout is frozen

earnings removed from eligibility queue

no instant payout allowed

cleaner cannot withdraw disputed funds

Once dispute is resolved:

credits are released according to the ruling

earnings become eligible

payout updates in ledger

---------------------------------------------------------
10. PAYOUT RATES: STANDARD & TIER-BASED
Cleaner tier determines earning multiplier:

Bronze (Tier 1)
lowest rate

highest platform fee

Silver (Tier 2)
moderate fee

moderate earning bump

Gold (Tier 3)
better payouts

priority jobs

Platinum (Tier 4)
top rate

lowest fee

instant payout priority

This aligns marketplace incentives → reliability = higher income.

Admins can:

✔ view payout logs

✔ override payout schedule
✔ force re-processing of payouts

Admins cannot:

✘ send payouts outside Stripe
✘ bypass fraud holds without documentation
✘ change historical job data

All admin actions create:

audit logs

timestamps

operator ID

reason code

---------------------------------------------------------
13. AUTOMATIONS INSIDE PAYOUT SYSTEM
Automation 1 — Weekly Batch Trigger
Runs at fixed time every week.

Automation 2 — Instant Payout Risk Scan
Before instant payout, the system runs:

identity check

balance verification

Automation 3 — Failed Payout Loop
If Stripe returns “Failed”:

notify cleaner

Automation 4 — Payout Eligibility Refresh
Runs hourly:

updates earnings list

removes disputed earnings

Excellent — continuing now with SECTION 3F — Tier System (Bronze → Platinum).

This is one of the most strategically important components of PureTask because:

it controls marketplace quality

=========================================================
3F — TIER SYSTEM (BRONZE → PLATINUM) (ULTRA-EXPANDED CANON)
=========================================================
PureTask uses a 4-level tier system:

Bronze — Entry Level

Silver — Consistent & Reliable

Gold — High Quality Professionals

Platinum — Elite, Top 5–10% of Cleaners

Tiers determine:

earning multipliers

platform fees

job visibility

search ranking

instant payout eligibility

access to premium jobs

client trust indicators

This system elevates cleaner behavior and maintains marketplace integrity.

---------------------------------------------------------
1. TIER OVERVIEW
Tier	Reliability Score Needed	Benefits	Risks
Bronze	0–69	Basic job access	High penalties, lowest payout
Silver	70–84	Standard access, better pay	Can drop back to Bronze
Gold	85–94	Priority ranking, higher pay	Must maintain high consistency
Platinum	95–100	Top visibility, lowest fees, instant payout priority	Hardest to maintain
Tiers are recalculated weekly.

---------------------------------------------------------
2. INPUTS INTO TIER CALCULATION
Tier is not based ONLY on reliability score.

It uses a weighted model:

Reliability Score (primary)

Photo Compliance Rate

On-Time Arrival Percentage

Dispute Rate

Cancellation Rate

Job Completion Count (to prevent new cleaners from jumping too fast)

Weight Breakdown Example:
Reliability Score → 60%

Photo Compliance → 15%

Punctuality → 10%

Dispute Rate → 10%

Cancellation Rate → 5%

The system uses these weights to produce a Tier Qualification Score.

---------------------------------------------------------
3. TIER SCORE BOUNDARIES
Bronze
0 – 69
Entry-level; limited benefits; higher platform fee.

Silver
70 – 84
Decent cleaners; consistency improving.

Gold
85 – 94
High-level cleaners; trusted by platform.

Platinum
95 – 100
Elite performance; high trust; priority in search.

---------------------------------------------------------
4. TIER BENEFITS (DETAILED)
Bronze Benefits
access to available jobs

ability to build up to Silver

lower expectations but higher guidance

Limitations:
lower pay rate

no premium job access

instant payout unavailable

lower search ranking

Silver Benefits
standard marketplace visibility

increased pay rate

improved ranking

access to more jobs

Limitations:
not prioritized for premium clients

instant payout still limited

Gold Benefits
priority job assignments

premium client access

higher earning potential

lower platform fee

instant payout unlocked

Gold cleaners make significantly more per hour.

Platinum Benefits
top ranking

early access to most profitable jobs

lowest platform fee

exclusive client segments

guaranteed instant payouts

“Elite Cleaner” badge on profile

considered for brand ambassador roles

---------------------------------------------------------
5. TIER PENALTIES
Tier drops occur when reliability score drops below a threshold:

Platinum → Gold
reliability < 95

or disputes occur

or late cancellations

Gold → Silver
reliability < 85

or multiple late arrivals

or photo compliance issues

Silver → Bronze
reliability < 70

serious performance decline

Tier changes trigger:

notification

guidance messages

tips for recovery

---------------------------------------------------------
6. EARNING MULTIPLIERS & PLATFORM FEE REDUCTIONS
Tier controls platform fee percentage.

Example model:

Tier	Cleaner Earnings	Platform Fee
Bronze	baseline rate	30%
Silver	+5–10%	25%
Gold	+15–20%	20%
Platinum	+25–30%	15%
Higher tiers = more money per hour.

This creates a strong incentive to maintain performance.

---------------------------------------------------------
7. JOB VISIBILITY & SEARCH RANKING LOGIC
When clients browse cleaners:

Platinum cleaners appear first
Sorted by:

reliability

reviews

distance

Gold appear next
Silver appear middle
Bronze appear last
If a client selects “Auto Assign Cleaner,” the algorithm prioritizes:

Platinum

Gold

Silver

Bronze (only if necessary)

---------------------------------------------------------

dispute rate

---------------------------------------------------------
9. TIER AUDIT SYSTEM (WEEKLY)
Every Sunday at 11:59 PM:

calculate tier qualification score

check dispute rate

evaluate cancellation patterns

examine photo compliance

review punctuality

determine new tier

Changes take effect immediately.

Cleaner receives:

Tier Up message
or

Tier Down message
or

“Maintain your tier” message

With personalized suggestions.

---------------------------------------------------------
10. TIER DECAY LOGIC (INACTIVITY RULES)
To prevent dormant cleaners from staying in high tiers:

If no jobs for 21 days:
reliability decays 5 points

tier may downgrade automatically

If no jobs for 45 days:
forced downgrade to Silver

If >60 days inactivity:
downgrade to Bronze

must complete 3 jobs successfully to unlock Silver again

---------------------------------------------------------
11. PHOTO COMPLIANCE IMPACT ON TIER
Photo compliance is a major trust indicator.

Rules:
90%+ compliant → boost

80–89% → neutral

<80% → penalty

<70% → automatic tier drop

<60% → reliability warning + suspension risk

This ensures the visual verification system stays consistent.

---------------------------------------------------------
12. DISPUTE RATE IMPACT ON TIER
Disputes heavily impact trust.

Tier rules:

1 dispute in 30 days → warning

2 disputes → reliability deduction

3 disputes → automatic downgrade

4 disputes → account under review

If disputes are client fraud → no penalty.

---------------------------------------------------------
13. CANCELLATION RATE IMPACT ON TIER
Cleaners who cancel often damage client trust.

Rules:

<5% cancellations → good

5–10% → small penalty

10–20% → tier risk

20% → automatic downgrade

repeated last-minute cancellations → heavy penalties

---------------------------------------------------------

Cleaner sees:

badge

progress toward next tier

Client sees:

badge

short explanation

trust indicator

Triggered when cleaner crosses threshold.

Automation 3: Tier Down Notification
Triggered when reliability drops.

Automation 4: “Near Tier Upgrade” Motivation
If cleaner is within 3–5 points of next tier.

If cancellation or dispute triggers tier review.

=========================================================
3G — RELIABILITY ENGINE (ULTRA-EXPANDED CANON)
=========================================================
The Reliability Engine is the algorithm that determines:

cleaner ranking

tier advancement

access to premium jobs

booking priority

platform fee reductions

instant payout eligibility

suspension triggers

trust indicators

client safety

marketplace stability

Reliability Score ranges from 0 → 100.

It dynamically adjusts after every job, event, or violation.

This system is the core of PureTask’s marketplace integrity.

Let’s expand every detail.

---------------------------------------------------------
1. PURPOSE OF RELIABILITY ENGINE
The Reliability Score exists to:

Encourage professional behavior

Reward cleaners who perform consistently

Discourage last-minute cancellations

Prevent fraud and system abuse

Protect clients from low-quality service

Reduce disputes

Increase cleaner earnings fairly

Create predictable marketplace performance

Power the tier system

Support auto-assignment logic

It is the true reputation metric of PureTask.

---------------------------------------------------------
2. CORE INPUTS INTO RELIABILITY SCORE
The system is fed by multiple event types:

⭐ Core Performance Inputs
On-time arrival

Photo compliance

Job completion

Client satisfaction

Time spent at job

Quality of before/after photos

⚠️ Penalty Inputs
Late arrivals

Missing photos

GPS anomalies

Cancellation behavior

No-shows

Dispute outcomes

Complaints

Behavior flags

🛡 Fraud & Safety Inputs
repeated metadata inconsistencies

repeat dispute patterns

client safety reports

suspicious GPS or device patterns

Each factor has weighted impact.

---------------------------------------------------------
3. RELIABILITY SCORE CALCULATION MODEL
Score starts at:

70 for new cleaners (Silver baseline)
Why not 100?
→ must earn trust, not inherit it.

Reliability adjusts per job.

Reliability Formula (conceptual version):
Reliability = BaseScore 
             + PositiveEvents 
             - NegativeEvents 
             - FraudFlags 
             - SafetyFlags 
             - CancellationPenalties
The actual algorithm is a weighted rolling average over the last X jobs (ex: 20 jobs).

Earlier jobs have less weight to avoid punishing long-term cleaners for past mistakes.

---------------------------------------------------------
4. POSITIVE EVENTS & POINT ADDITIONS
These reward consistency and professionalism.

On-Time Arrival
5 points
(+8 if 10+ consecutive punctual jobs)

Perfect Photo Compliance
5 points

5-Star Client Rating
3 points

Cleaner Adds Helpful Notes
1 point (quality signal)

Zero Disputes for 10 Jobs
4 bonus points

Client Saves Cleaner to Favorites
2 point trust boost

Client Rebooks Cleaner
2 points

Platinum-Eligible Behaviors
flawless GPS streak (15+ jobs) → +5

dispute-free streak for 30 days → +7

Positive events are capped to prevent inflating scores endlessly:
Max score: 100

---------------------------------------------------------
5. NEGATIVE EVENTS & PENALTIES
These are more impactful because reliability is a trust metric.

❌ Late Arrival (0–15 min)
-5 points

❌ Late Arrival (>15 min)
-10 points

❌ Missing Before Photos
-15 points

❌ Missing After Photos
-15 points

❌ Poor-Quality Photos
(blurry, dark, badly framed)
-5 to -8 points

❌ Partial Job Completion
-20 points

❌ Cleaner Cancels <24 Hours
-25 points

❌ Cleaner Cancels <3 Hours
-40 points

❌ No-Show Without Notice
-50 points
(Instant suspension)

❌ Client Complaints
-5 to -15 depending on severity

---------------------------------------------------------
6. DISPUTE IMPACT ON RELIABILITY
Disputes influence trust heavily.

Dispute filed but resolved FOR cleaner
No penalty

+3 bonus points (vindicated case)

Dispute resolved PARTIAL
-5 points

Dispute resolved AGAINST cleaner
-20 points

Repeated disputes
3 disputes in 30 days → auto reliability drop into Bronze zone

5 disputes in 60 days → platform review

---------------------------------------------------------
7. GPS & CHECK-IN RELIABILITY FACTORS
GPS is a core trust signal.

Perfect GPS streak (10+ jobs)
+3 points

GPS Inconsistency
-10 points

Suspicious location patterns
-20 points
(triggers internal fraud investigation)

GPS Spoofing
-100 reliability
Instant permanent ban.

---------------------------------------------------------
8. CANCELLATION BEHAVIOR WEIGHTING
Cleaners who cancel often disrupt client trust.

Cancel >24 hours
0 penalty

Cancel <24 hours
-15 to -25 points

Cancel <3 hours
-25 to -40 points

Repeated cancellations
3 cancellations in 30 days → -40
5 cancellations in 60 days → -70 and temp suspension

---------------------------------------------------------
9. RELIABILITY DECAY & RECOVERY RULES
🚫 Decay Rules
Applied for inactivity:

No jobs in 21 days → -5 points

No jobs in 45 days → -15 points

No jobs in 60 days → automatic drop to Bronze

Purpose:

ensures the score reflects active performance

prevents stale metrics from misrepresenting skill

⭐ Recovery Rules
For cleaners who improve:

+10 points for completing 5 perfect jobs

+20 points for 10 perfect jobs

+30 points for 20 perfect jobs

Cleaners can repair their standing through consistent performance.

---------------------------------------------------------
10. RELIABILITY → TIER MAPPING
Reliability is the primary determinant of tier.

Reliability Score	Tier	Meaning
95–100	Platinum	Elite cleaner
85–94	Gold	Highly trusted
70–84	Silver	Stable performer
<70	Bronze	Needs improvement
<50	Probation zone	Suspension risk
<30	Suspended	Must be reviewed

higher in client search

more often in “recommended cleaners”

notify admin

require review

Automation 5 — Fraud Tagging
If photos or GPS patterns match fraud signatures:

reliability drops

payout freeze

---------------------------------------------------------
14. RELIABILITY ALERT SYSTEM
Cleaners receive real-time alerts:

🚨 Warning Alerts
“Your reliability dropped to 78 due to late arrival.”

“Missing photos resulted in a penalty.”

⭐ Positive Feedback Alerts
“Nice job! Your last job improved your reliability score.”

🛟 Coaching & Guidance
automated suggestions to improve reliability

1. Client leaves unfair negative review
Admin may adjust reliability if evidence disproves complaint.

2. Cleaner claims GPS malfunction
Admin can override penalties if proof supports claim.

3. Multi-dispute house
If multiple cleaners dispute the SAME client:

client gets flagged

cleaner penalties reversed

4. Sudden reliability drop
If reliability drops more than 30 points in 24 hours:

auto investigation triggered

Understood — proceeding now with SECTION 3H — Dispute System (Ultra-Expanded Canon).

This is one of the most sensitive, carefully engineered systems in the entire PureTask platform because it directly influences:

client trust

cleaner fairness

payouts

marketplace stability

fraud prevention

photo requirements

GPS verification

reliability scoring

admin workload

long-term platform health

A dispute system that is too harsh → cleaners flee.
A dispute system that is too soft → clients lose trust.
A dispute system that is unclear → chaos.

PureTask needs a balanced, evidence-driven, transparent, fair, and automated dispute system.

Let’s build it.

=========================================================
3H — DISPUTE SYSTEM (ULTRA-EXPANDED CANON)
=========================================================
A dispute occurs when a client does not approve a completed job, citing that the cleaning was not done to expectations.

The dispute system must:

protect clients from incomplete work

protect cleaners from unfair complaints

rely on evidence only (photos, GPS, notes, timestamps)

be fast, consistent, and unbiased

enforce rules of professionalism

maintain marketplace trust

A well-designed dispute system reduces:

refund abuse

fraudulent cleaners

cleaner turnover

client dissatisfaction

Let’s break everything down.

---------------------------------------------------------
1. WHEN A DISPUTE CAN BE OPENED
Clients may open a dispute ONLY under specific conditions:

✔ After cleaner submits all photos
✔ Before they approve the job
✔ Within the dispute window (ex: 24 hours after completion)
Clients can dispute for:

Missing areas

Poor-quality cleaning

Incomplete job

Cleaner left early

Areas not addressed as instructed

Damage during job

Cleaner behavior issues

Safety concerns

Misuse of home or belongings

Fraudulent activity (fake check-in, fake photos)

Clients CANNOT dispute for:

price disagreement

“I changed my mind”

personal preference after approval

issues unrelated to cleaning

off-platform communication

extra tasks not included in service

---------------------------------------------------------
2. CLIENT DISPUTE FLOW (UX + LOGIC)
Step 1 — Client selects “Open Dispute”
Prompt:
“What issue did you experience with your cleaning?”

Categories:

Missed area(s)

Poor cleaning quality

Cleaner left early

Instructions not followed

Something was damaged

Safety/behavior issue

Other (describe)

Step 2 — Client selects evidence
They must choose items from:

before photos

after photos

markup tools (optional future feature)

text explanation

highlight areas of concern

Step 3 — System checks evidence validity
Ex:
If client says “Bathroom not cleaned” but after photos show a clean bathroom → system flags inconsistency.

Step 4 — Dispute submitted
Escrow is frozen.
Cleaner is notified instantly.

Status changes to: DISPUTED

---------------------------------------------------------
3. CLEANER DISPUTE RESPONSE FLOW
Cleaners have the right to respond.

Cleaner options:

Option 1 — Accept fault
Cleaner acknowledges mistake.
Partial or full refund possible.
Cleaner receives slight penalty.

Option 2 — Provide justification
Cleaner provides:

explanation

photo evidence

time logs

notes on instructions

issues encountered

Option 3 — Offer re-clean (policy dependent)
Cleaner returns to fix the issue.

Cleaner cannot:

contact client outside the app

intimidate the client

request the client approve regardless

upload new fake photos

modify timestamps

Cleaner has X hours to respond (ex: 12 hours).

If cleaner doesn’t respond → admin resolves with client evidence.

---------------------------------------------------------
4. ADMIN RESOLUTION WORKFLOW
Admin sees a complete case file:

Evidence Displayed:
before photos

after photos

metadata

GPS timestamps

cleaner check-in/out times

client complaint

cleaner response

reliability history

dispute history

job notes

home profile

previous ratings at this address

Admin Tools:
zoom on photos

side-by-side comparison

brightness enhancement

EXIF metadata viewer

time comparison tools

checklist reference

Admin must determine:
Was the job completed?

Is the complaint legitimate?

Did cleaner violate any rules?

Is there any fraud?

Is the client being unfair?

What percentage (if any) should be refunded?

---------------------------------------------------------
5. POSSIBLE DISPUTE OUTCOMES
Admin can choose:

Outcome 1 — Full Release to Cleaner (0% refund)
Reasons:

photos clearly show job was completed

client complaint invalid

client trying to misuse dispute system

Cleaner:

no penalty

+3 reliability boost

Client:

receives educational message about evidence

system flags possible abuse if repeated

Outcome 2 — Partial Refund (20–80%)
Reasons:

some areas incomplete

unclear cleaning in a room

photos missing for part of job

minor quality issues

Cleaner:

loses some earnings

reliability -5 to -15 depending on severity

Client:

refunded portion of credits

Outcome 3 — Full Refund (100%)
Reasons:

cleaner missed entire rooms

no before/after photos

cleaner left early

incomplete work proven

cleaner behavior issue

fraud

safety concern

Cleaner:

heavy penalty (-20 to -50 reliability)

possible suspension

Client:

refunded fully

invited to rebook

Outcome 4 — Offer Re-Clean
Cleaner may return to fix issues.
This option is not always used because:

clients may not want the same cleaner to return

timing may not work

disputes prolong payment delays

But is allowed in some cases.

---------------------------------------------------------
6. HOW DISPUTES AFFECT RELIABILITY
If resolved in cleaner’s favor:
no penalty

+3 bonus

If partial refund:
-5 to -15 points

If full refund issued:
-20 to -50 points

Repeated disputes:
3 disputes in 30 days → major tier risk

5 disputes in 60 days → account review

7+ disputes lifetime → flagged for coaching

Cleaners are protected from unfair disputes because decisions rely on evidence, not emotions.

---------------------------------------------------------
7. SYSTEM AUTOMATIONS FOR DISPUTES
Automation 1 — Evidence Package Assembly
Automatically gathers:

photos

metadata

GPS

timestamps

Automation 2 — Fraud Pattern Detection
Flags:

repeated missed angle patterns

edited photos

metadata mismatch

duplicate photo uploads

Automation 3 — Auto-Decision (Low-Complexity Cases)
Examples:

missing photos → auto partial refund

no check-in → auto refund

client complaint invalid → auto-approve

Auto-decisions reduce admin workload.

Automation 4 — Client Dispute Limit System
Clients who dispute excessively:

flagged

required evidence increased

dispute privileges temporarily restricted

Threshold example:

3 disputes in 60 days

or >2 disputes rejected as invalid

Automation 5 — Cleaner Coaching Trigger
If cleaner loses 2 disputes in 30 days:

trigger training module

send behavior guidance

forward case for quality review

Automation 6 — Earnings Freeze
While dispute is open:

earnings locked

no instant payout

job removed from earning queue

---------------------------------------------------------
8. SPECIAL DISPUTE CATEGORIES
Category A — Behavior Issues
Includes:

unprofessional behavior

hostile tone

inappropriate comments

unsafe actions

Penalty range:
-20 to -60 reliability
Possible ban.

Category B — Damage Claims
Rare but serious.

Verification:

timestamped photos

client video

cleaner notes

before/after correlation

If cleaner at fault:

client partially compensated

cleaner reliability severely impacted

potential suspension

Category C — Safety Concerns
Includes:

intoxication

dangerous behavior

harassment

unauthorized areas entered

Outcome:

immediate suspension pending review

Category D — Cleaner Fraud
Includes:

fake photos

GPS spoofing

staged before/after sets

Outcome:

full refund

permanent ban

reliability set to 0

payout freeze

Category E — Client Fraud
Includes:

lying about incomplete job

modifying the home after photos

staging mess after cleaning

disputing to avoid paying

Outcome:

client warning

dispute denied

account review

possible suspension

---------------------------------------------------------
9. DISPUTE TIME LIMITS
Client must dispute within:
24 hours of job completion

Cleaner must respond within:
12 hours (recommended)

Admin must resolve within:
24–48 hours

If client does nothing:

job auto-approved

If cleaner does nothing:

admin rules based on client evidence

---------------------------------------------------------
10. UI & COMMUNICATION RULES
Client UI Messages:
clear

calm

non-accusatory

evidence-driven

Example:
“Thank you — we will review your photos and get back to you shortly.”

Cleaner UI Messages:
accountability-focused

factual

constructive

Example:
“Please review the client’s concern and provide your response within 12 hours.”

---------------------------------------------------------
11. EDGE CASES
Case 1 — Client disappears
Auto-approval occurs.

Case 2 — Cleaner disappears
Admin resolves based on evidence.

Case 3 — No photos at all
Cleaner receives full penalty.
Client refunded.

Case 4 — Photos unclear
Cleaner asked to clarify.
Dispute escalates.

Case 5 — Job took far less time than estimated
If cleaning still complete → no penalty
If work incomplete → partial refund

Case 6 — Client asks for tasks not included
Cleaner is protected.
Dispute invalid.

=========================================================
⭐ 3H COMPLETE — FULL DISPUTE SYSTEM CANON
=========================================================
Next:

3I — Notification System (Ultra-Expanded)
Includes:

all email, SMS & push templates

triggers

critical alerts

job lifecycle messages

payout notifications

dispute notifications

tone rules

fallback logic

redundancy mechanisms

This is the communication backbone of PureTask.

=========================================================
3I — NOTIFICATION SYSTEM (ULTRA-EXPANDED CANON)
=========================================================
PureTask uses a multi-channel notification system to guarantee:

cleaners never miss jobs

clients are always informed

dispute and payout processes move quickly

compliance is maintained

reliability is improved automatically

the marketplace feels alive and responsive

Notifications are part of the core product experience, not an afterthought.

The notification system consists of:

Push Notifications

SMS

Email

In-App Banners

In-App Alerts

System Reminders (Automated)

Critical Interrupt Alerts

All notifications follow PureTask’s tone rules:

Calm

Neutral

Helpful

Direct

Non-emotional

No fear-based language

No blame assignment

No aggressive tone

---------------------------------------------------------
1. NOTIFICATION CHANNELS & RULES
Push Notifications
Primary channel for all real-time updates.

Used for:

job confirmations

check-in reminders

photo reminders

dispute alerts

payout notifications

tier updates

Rules:

short

actionable

never emotional

avoid long explanations

SMS Messages
Used for:

critical alerts

failed push fallback

time-sensitive events (check-in overdue, payout failed)

Rules:

must be concise

no links unless necessary

SMS used sparingly

Emails
Used for:

receipts

dispute summaries

payout confirmations

account updates

onboarding flows

low urgency but important details

Emails are longer, more structured, and branding-aligned.

In-App Banners
Used for:

soft reminders

tier progress nudges

upcoming job reminders

missing profile details

In-App Alerts (modal popups)
Used for:

urgent compliance items

missing photos

missing check-in

dispute deadlines

payout setup issues

Critical Interrupt Alerts
Used ONLY for:

safety issues

payout failures

repeated GPS failures

potential fraud

account suspension

Critical alerts bypass silent mode and must be acknowledged.

---------------------------------------------------------
2. NOTIFICATION TYPES (FULL MATRIX)
PureTask sends 34 categories of notifications.

Below is the full list.

A. Booking Notifications
Booking Confirmed (Client)
“Your cleaning is booked. Your cleaner will check in upon arrival.”

Booking Assigned (Cleaner)
“You’ve been assigned a new job for tomorrow at [time].”

Booking Reminder — 24 hours (Client + Cleaner)
“You have a cleaning scheduled for tomorrow.”

Booking Reminder — 1 hour (Client + Cleaner)
“Your cleaning is starting soon.”

Cleaner Match Updated (Client)
“A new cleaner has been assigned to your job.”

Job Canceled (Client)
“Your upcoming cleaning has been canceled.”

Cleaner Cancelled (Client)
“Your cleaner can no longer make it. We are finding a replacement.”

B. Check-In Notifications
Check-In Time Window Opening
“Your check-in window is now open.”

Cleaner Late Reminder (Cleaner)
“You are past the scheduled time. Please check in immediately.”

Check-In Confirmed (Client)
“Your cleaner has arrived and checked in.”

GPS Error / Location Issue
“We could not verify your location. Please retry check-in.”

C. Photo Proof Notifications
Before Photo Reminder
“Please upload before photos to continue this job.”

After Photo Reminder
“Please upload after photos to complete this job.”

Poor-Quality Photo Warning
“Some photos are unclear. Please retake them.”

Client: Photos Ready
“Your cleaning photos are ready for review.”

D. Job Completion Notifications
Cleaner Completed Job (Client)
“Your cleaner has submitted the job for your review.”

Review Reminder (Client)
“Please review the cleaning photos to approve this job.”

Auto-Approval Warning (Client)
“This job will auto-approve soon. Please review the photos.”

E. Disputes & Issues
Dispute Opened (Cleaner)
“A dispute was opened regarding today’s cleaning.”

Dispute Response Needed (Cleaner)
“Please respond to the dispute within 12 hours.”

Dispute Resolved (Both)
“Your dispute has been resolved. View details in the app.”

Client Dispute Received (Admin Copy)
Automatically logs dispute for admin review.

Evidence Submitted Reminder
(Client or cleaner must send additional information)

F. Payout Notifications
Earnings Added
“Your earnings from this job are now available.”

Weekly Payout Sent
“Your payout has been sent to your bank.”

Instant Payout Sent
“Your instant payout was successful.”

Payout Failed
“Your payout could not be completed. Update your bank details.”

Payout On Hold
“Your payout is temporarily on hold while we review your account.”

G. Tier & Reliability Notifications
Tier Upgrade
“Congratulations! You’re now a Gold Cleaner.”

Tier Downgrade
“Your tier has changed based on recent activity.”

Reliability Drop Warning
“Your reliability score has decreased to 78.”

Reliability Improvement
“Great job! Your reliability increased after your last job.”

H. Profile & Compliance
Profile Incomplete
“Please complete your profile to receive more jobs.”

Verification Needed
“Your identity verification needs action.”

---------------------------------------------------------
3. MESSAGE TONE RULES (STRICT)
All notifications MUST follow PureTask’s tone rules:

🚫 Forbidden Tone:
aggressive

panicked

overly emotional

accusatory

passive aggressive

slang-heavy

guilt-inducing

✔ Required Tone:
neutral

factual

calm

professional

clear & short

supportive

Examples:

❌ Bad:
“You’re late again! This is unacceptable!”

✔ Good:
“You are past the scheduled start time. Please check in as soon as possible.”

---------------------------------------------------------
4. CLIENT & CLEANER NOTIFICATION FLOWS BY LIFECYCLE
Here is the full notification flow mapped to the job lifecycle.

Phase 1: Booking
“Booking Confirmed” (client)

“New Job Assigned” (cleaner)

Phase 2: Pre-Job Reminders
24-hour reminder

1-hour reminder

Phase 3: Arrival
“Check-In Window Open” (cleaner)

“Cleaner Checked In” (client)

Phase 4: Photo Submission
before photo reminders

after photo reminders

Phase 5: Job Completion
“Cleaner submitted job”

“Photos ready for review”

Phase 6: Approval
“Review Reminder”

“Auto-approval soon”

Phase 7: Payout
“Earnings Added”

“Instant payout successful” or “Payout sent”

Phase 8: Disputes
dispute opened

response required

dispute resolved

---------------------------------------------------------
5. FAILOVER LOGIC (FALLBACK RULES)
Push notifications are NOT enough.
PureTask must ensure deliverability.

If Push Fails → SMS
Triggered when:

push notification fails

user hasn’t opened the app in 2+ hours

critical event is happening (check-in, dispute, payout issue)

If SMS fails → Email
Used as backup for:

payout failures

disputes

verification issues

If ALL channels fail
A compliance banner appears on next login.

---------------------------------------------------------
6. HIGH-URGENCY NOTIFICATIONS (CRITICAL ALERTS)
These override silence modes (within reason):

cleaner no-show

payout failure

GPS spoof detection

high-severity disputes

repeated missed photos

account suspension

client safety report

Tone remains calm, but delivery is immediate.

---------------------------------------------------------
7. AUTOMATION TRIGGERS (BACKEND)
Automation 1 — Job Assignment
Triggers push + SMS (cleaner).

Automation 2 — Check-In Reminder
Triggered if cleaner not checked in X minutes after start time.

Automation 3 — Missing Photo Reminder
Triggered every 10 minutes until completed (limit 4 reminders).

Automation 4 — Auto-Approval Timer
Triggers warning 2 hours before auto-approval.

Automation 5 — Dispute Clock
If cleaner does not respond within 12 hours → admin escalation.

Automation 6 — Payout Batch
Weekly payout triggers email + push.

Automation 7 — Profile Incompletion
Triggered 48 hours after incomplete onboarding.

---------------------------------------------------------
8. TONE SAMPLES & MESSAGE TEMPLATES (SELECT EXAMPLES)
Here are a few canonical template examples:

Booking Confirmed
“Your cleaning is booked. Your cleaner will check in when they arrive.”

Check-In Reminder
“Your check-in time has arrived. Please check in when you are at the job location.”

Photo Reminder
“Please upload your before photos to continue your job.”

Review Reminder
“Please review the cleaning photos to complete the job.”

Dispute Alert
“A dispute has been opened for this job. Please review the details.”

Payout Success
“Your payout has been sent to your bank.”

job paused

grace period applied

3. Cleaner forgets before photos
reliability penalty

client may dispute

may require admin override

Photos/videos stored locally until connection restored.

5. Cleaner leaves early
System compares:

expected duration

photo timestamps

GPS exit time
